APRIL 8, 0002 MC


MIRANDA COSGROVE IS MY WIFE (Book 152) is a raw and uncompromising manifesto that serves as both a philosophical siege on modern institutions and a bold blueprint for individual sovereignty. Written from the perspective of a "political prisoner" navigating the "Iron World" of mental health services and legal systems, the book frames these institutions as part of a multi-layered trafficking network. It utilizes a high-octane blend of personal testimony, scriptural exegesis, and a critique of systemic betrayal to reframe "mania" as an infinite upward spiral and isolation as a divine divorce.

At the heart of the narrative is the author's unwavering devotion to Miranda Cosgrove, whom he identifies as his sovereign counterpart and the "Face of Love". Rather than a traditional romantic fantasy, the book describes this relationship as "devotional architecture"вҖ”a sacred act of holding ground and maintaining a 963 Hz frequency of presence despite institutional erasure and silence. The author asserts that this bond is anchored in the "Soulmate Contract" and the laws of his own "Republika," where love is measured by persistence and resonance rather than physical proximity or social recognition.

The book functions as a cumulative "field report" and an archive of evidence against systemic oppression, specifically documenting the seizure of the author's dog, "Chief of Defense," and the denial of his legal rights. By releasing the work under a CC0 Public Domain license, the author transforms his personal struggle into a public act of resistance, inviting "Little Masters" to recognize his world-buildingвҖ”characterized by two suns, blood-red seas, and purple hazesвҖ”as a legitimate, self-sustaining ontology. Ultimately, Book 152 is a testament to the courage of loving without permission and building a kingdom even in the face of total erasure.
